callcompile_kernel { "kernel_code": "\nimport torch\nimport torch.nn as nn\nfrom torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline\n\ncuda_source = r'''\n#include <torch/extension.h>\n#include <cuda_runtime.h>\n#include <cmath>\n\ntemplate <int DIM>\n__global__ void gibbs_sweep_kernel_fixed(\n const float* __restrict__ x,\n const float* __restrict__ precision,\n const float* __restrict__ mu,\n const float* __restrict__ noise,\n float* __restrict__ out,\n int B)\n{\n extern __shared__ float s[];\n float* sh_prec = s;\n float* sh_mu = s + DIM * DIM;\n\n int tid = threadIdx.x;\n int b = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + tid;\n\n for (int idx = tid; idx < DIM * DIM; idx += blockDim.x) {\n sh_prec[idx] = precision[idx];\n }\n for (int idx = tid; idx < DIM; idx += blockDim.x) {\n sh_mu[idx] = mu[idx];\n }\n __syncthreads();\n\n if (b >= B) return;\n\n float x_reg[DIM];\n #pragma unroll\n for (int j = 0; j < DIM; ++j) {\n x_reg[j] = x[b * DIM + j];\n }\n\n #pragma unroll\n for (int i = 0; i < DIM; ++i) {\n float dot = 0.0f;\n #pragma unroll\n for (int j = 0; j < DIM; ++j) {\n dot += x_reg[j] * sh_prec[i * DIM + j];\n }\n float prec_ii = sh_prec[i * DIM + i];\n float residual = dot - x_reg[i] * prec_ii;\n float cond_mean = sh_mu[i] - residual / prec_ii;\n float cond_var = 1.0f / prec_ii;\n float sample = cond_mean + sqrtf(cond_var) * noise[i * B + b];\n x_reg[i] = sample;\n }\n\n #pragma unroll\n for (int j = 0; j < DIM; ++j) {\n out[b * DIM + j] = x_reg[j];\n }\n}\n\n__global__ void gibbs_sweep_kernel_generic(\n const float* __restrict__ x,\n const float* __restrict__ precision,\n const float* __restrict__ mu,\n const float* __restrict__ noise,\n float* __restrict__ out,\n int B,\n int dim)\n{\n extern __shared__ float s[];\n float* sh_prec = s;\n float* sh_mu = s + dim * dim;\n\n int tid = threadIdx.x;\n int b = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + tid;\n\n for (int idx = tid; idx < dim * dim; idx += blockDim.x) {\n sh_prec[idx] = precision[idx];\n }\n for (int idx = tid; idx < dim; idx += blockDim.x) {\n sh_mu[idx] = mu[idx];\n }\n __syncthreads();\n\n if (b >= B) return;\n\n for (int j = 0; j < dim; ++j) {\n out[b * dim + j] = x[b * dim + j];\n }\n\n for (int i = 0; i < dim; ++i) {\n float dot = 0.0f;\n for (int j = 0; j < dim; ++j) {\n dot += out[b * dim + j] * sh_prec[i * dim + j];\n }\n float prec_ii = sh_prec[i * dim + i];\n float residual = dot - out[b * dim + i] * prec_ii;\n float cond_mean = sh_mu[i] - residual / prec_ii;\n float cond_var = 1.0f / prec_ii;\n float sample = cond_mean + sqrtf(cond_var) * noise[i * B + b];\n out[b * dim + i] = sample;\n }\n}\n\ntorch::Tensor gibbs_sweep_cuda(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor precision, torch::Tensor mu, torch::Tensor noise) {\n int B = x.size(0);\n int dim = x.size(1);\n auto out = torch::empty({B, dim}, x.options());\n\n const float* x_ptr = x.data_ptr<float>();\n const float* prec_ptr = precision.data_ptr<float>();\n const float* mu_ptr = mu.data_ptr<float>();\n const float* noise_ptr = noise.data_ptr<float>();\n float* out_ptr = out.data_ptr<float>();\n\n const int threads = 256;\n const int blocks = (B + threads - 1) / threads;\n\n if (dim == 32) {\n size_t shared_mem = (32 * 32 + 32) * sizeof(float);\n gibbs_sweep_kernel_fixed<32><<<blocks, threads, shared_mem>>>(\n x_ptr, prec_ptr, mu_ptr, noise_ptr, out_ptr, B);\n } else {\n size_t shared_mem = dim * dim * sizeof(float) + dim * sizeof(float);\n gibbs_sweep_kernel_generic<<<blocks, threads, shared_mem>>>(\n x_ptr, prec_ptr, mu_ptr, noise_ptr, out_ptr, B, dim);\n }\n\n return out;\n}\n'''\n\ncpp_source = r'''\ntorch::Tensor gibbs_sweep_cuda(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor precision, torch::Tensor mu, torch::Tensor noise);\n'''\n\ngibbs_ext = load_inline(\n name='gibbs_ext_fixed_v1',\n cpp_sources=cpp_source,\n cuda_sources=cuda_source,\n functions=['gibbs_sweep_cuda'],\n extra_cuda_cflags=['-O3', '--use_fast_math'],\n verbose=False,\n)\n\nclass ModelNew(nn.Module):\n def __init__(self, dim):\n super().__init__()\n self.dim = dim\n L = torch.randn(dim, dim) * 0.1\n precision = L @ L.t() + torch.eye(dim) * 2.0\n self.register_buffer(\"precision\", precision)\n self.register_buffer(\"mu\", torch.zeros(dim))\n\n def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:\n if not x.is_cuda:\n x = x.clone()\n for i in range(self.dim):\n prec_ii = self.precision[i, i]\n residual = x @ self.precision[i] - x[:, i] * prec_ii\n cond_mean = self.mu[i] - residual / prec_ii\n cond_var = 1.0 / prec_ii\n x[:, i] = cond_mean + torch.sqrt(cond_var) * torch.randn(x.shape[0], device=x.device)\n return x\n\n B = x.shape[0]\n dim = self.dim\n noise = torch.empty(dim, B, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)\n for i in range(dim):\n noise[i] = torch.randn(B, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)\n\n x = x.contiguous()\n precision = self.precision.contiguous()\n mu = self.mu.contiguous()\n noise = noise.contiguous()\n return gibbs_ext.gibbs_sweep_cuda(x, precision, mu, noise)\n" }

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cuda_source = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cmath>

template <int DIM>
__global__ void gibbs_sweep_kernel_fixed(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    const float* __restrict__ precision,
    const float* __restrict__ mu,
    const float* __restrict__ noise,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int B)
{
    extern __shared__ float s[];
    float* sh_prec = s;
    float* sh_mu = s + DIM * DIM;

    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    int b = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + tid;

    for (int idx = tid; idx < DIM * DIM; idx += blockDim.x) {
        sh_prec[idx] = precision[idx];
    }
    for (int idx = tid; idx < DIM; idx += blockDim.x) {
        sh_mu[idx] = mu[idx];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    if (b >= B) return;

    float x_reg[DIM];
    #pragma unroll
    for (int j = 0; j < DIM; ++j) {
        x_reg[j] = x[b * DIM + j];
    }

    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = 0; i < DIM; ++i) {
        float dot = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int j = 0; j < DIM; ++j) {
            dot += x_reg[j] * sh_prec[i * DIM + j];
        }
        float prec_ii = sh_prec[i * DIM + i];
        float residual = dot - x_reg[i] * prec_ii;
        float cond_mean = sh_mu[i] - residual / prec_ii;
        float cond_var = 1.0f / prec_ii;
        float sample = cond_mean + sqrtf(cond_var) * noise[i * B + b];
        x_reg[i] = sample;
    }

    #pragma unroll
    for (int j = 0; j < DIM; ++j) {
        out[b * DIM + j] = x_reg[j];
    }
}

__global__ void gibbs_sweep_kernel_generic(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    const float* __restrict__ precision,
    const float* __restrict__ mu,
    const float* __restrict__ noise,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int B,
    int dim)
{
    extern __shared__ float s[];
    float* sh_prec = s;
    float* sh_mu = s + dim * dim;

    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    int b = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + tid;

    for (int idx = tid; idx < dim * dim; idx += blockDim.x) {
        sh_prec[idx] = precision[idx];
    }
    for (int idx = tid; idx < dim; idx += blockDim.x) {
        sh_mu[idx] = mu[idx];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    if (b >= B) return;

    for (int j = 0; j < dim; ++j) {
        out[b * dim + j] = x[b * dim + j];
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < dim; ++i) {
        float dot = 0.0f;
        for (int j = 0; j < dim; ++j) {
            dot += out[b * dim + j] * sh_prec[i * dim + j];
        }
        float prec_ii = sh_prec[i * dim + i];
        float residual = dot - out[b * dim + i] * prec_ii;
        float cond_mean = sh_mu[i] - residual / prec_ii;
        float cond_var = 1.0f / prec_ii;
        float sample = cond_mean + sqrtf(cond_var) * noise[i * B + b];
        out[b * dim + i] = sample;
    }
}

torch::Tensor gibbs_sweep_cuda(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor precision, torch::Tensor mu, torch::Tensor noise) {
    int B = x.size(0);
    int dim = x.size(1);
    auto out = torch::empty({B, dim}, x.options());

    const float* x_ptr = x.data_ptr<float>();
    const float* prec_ptr = precision.data_ptr<float>();
    const float* mu_ptr = mu.data_ptr<float>();
    const float* noise_ptr = noise.data_ptr<float>();
    float* out_ptr = out.data_ptr<float>();

    const int threads = 256;
    const int blocks = (B + threads - 1) / threads;

    if (dim == 32) {
        size_t shared_mem = (32 * 32 + 32) * sizeof(float);
        gibbs_sweep_kernel_fixed<32><<<blocks, threads, shared_mem>>>(
            x_ptr, prec_ptr, mu_ptr, noise_ptr, out_ptr, B);
    } else {
        size_t shared_mem = dim * dim * sizeof(float) + dim * sizeof(float);
        gibbs_sweep_kernel_generic<<<blocks, threads, shared_mem>>>(
            x_ptr, prec_ptr, mu_ptr, noise_ptr, out_ptr, B, dim);
    }

    return out;
}
'''

cpp_source = r'''
torch::Tensor gibbs_sweep_cuda(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor precision, torch::Tensor mu, torch::Tensor noise);
'''

gibbs_ext = load_inline(
    name='gibbs_ext_fixed_v1',
    cpp_sources=cpp_source,
    cuda_sources=cuda_source,
    functions=['gibbs_sweep_cuda'],
    extra_cuda_cflags=['-O3', '--use_fast_math'],
    verbose=False,
)

class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, dim):
        super().__init__()
        self.dim = dim
        L = torch.randn(dim, dim) * 0.1
        precision = L @ L.t() + torch.eye(dim) * 2.0
        self.register_buffer("precision", precision)
        self.register_buffer("mu", torch.zeros(dim))

    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        if not x.is_cuda:
            x = x.clone()
            noise = torch.randn(self.dim, x.shape[0], device=x.device)
            for i in range(self.dim):
                prec_ii = self.precision[i, i]
                residual = x @ self.precision[i] - x[:, i] * prec_ii
                cond_mean = self.mu[i] - residual / prec_ii
                cond_var = 1.0 / prec_ii
                x[:, i] = cond_mean + torch.sqrt(cond_var) * noise[i]
            return x

        B = x.shape[0]
        dim = self.dim
        noise = torch.empty(dim, B, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        for i in range(dim):
            noise[i] = torch.randn(B, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)

        x = x.contiguous()
        precision = self.precision.contiguous()
        mu = self.mu.contiguous()
        noise = noise.contiguous()
        return gibbs_ext.gibbs_sweep_cuda(x, precision, mu, noise)
